<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="Hdh5R9GpYKBt">
 Sending International Transfers
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="vx7vJFj7vqcf">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Currency Functionality:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1npXX1vVcHtV">
  All the 3 major currencies
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   (USD, EUR, GBP)
  </strong>
  will go by
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   default
  </strong>
  through
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT
  </strong>
  .
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="0bmrgJEFW7ld">
  Other currencies (AUD, EGP. INR. CNY. etc.….) will go through
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   WISE
  </strong>
  by default.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="NGyrZ1YxQnFC">
  Customers can send international transfers through
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT
  </strong>
  using
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   AED
  </strong>
  account or
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   multi-currency
  </strong>
  account.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="uVHNXfMb4dJ4">
  Only difference for multi-currency account - customer will get to choose which account to initiate the SWIFT payment from
  <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
   (see below screenshots)
  </u>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3jZhuPlbt8kZ">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Important note:
  </strong>
  If customer can only find 3 currencies through available currencies list, that would mean he was
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   rejected
  </strong>
  by WISE, and will be allowed
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   only
  </strong>
  to send transfer through SWIFT (USD, EUR, GBP)
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="9P11PvE77yEJ">
  Refer to below links for more information about currency specific availability for each country.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="epytdRKppLfV">
  Only refer to
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT
  </strong>
  available currencies
  <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
   <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/c96fa992-52ca-4f74-b1af-c0d4fd7a4f2b" style="width:16px" width="16"/>
  </span>
  <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://wiobank.atlassian.net/l/cp/4y79QzZQ" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits - OPS
   </strong>
  </a>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="LlDqPR77jNvV">
  Refer to
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   WISE
  </strong>
  Available Currencies and limits
  <a class="ghq-card-content__file" data-ghq-card-content-filename="" data-ghq-card-content-type="FILE" href="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/b1f4a622-baa3-4162-8a51-0769b5a9bed4" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
   Currency coverage and limits (1).xlsx
  </a>
 </li>
</ul>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="Fd6pP4tfw2dp">
</h2>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="U3hiVJQdbtX7">
 Wise vs SWIFT Transfers
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="lzJJj8NLjNXo">
</p>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="480" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:480px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="wLr4WrLcBJ9Y">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Wise Transfers
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="ZzmEu5hlXS65">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        What is Wise?
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="SbHNrJiDzVnt">
        A partner of Wio to initiate outward international transfers in local currencies for +40 countries.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="vX5Rf37d0RDx">
        Formerly known as TransferWise
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="j9SLj9dCnJ4j">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Wise help Centre:
        </strong>
        <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://wise.com/help/" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
         Hi, how can we help? | Wise Help Centre
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="f8FzHRrdBnVI">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Internal only:
        </strong>
        Wise onboarding (sign-up) will only happen in the backend system and doesn't require any action from customer side.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="n1DbXlvddGJr">
        In case
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         WISE
        </strong>
        rejected the customer account for any reason, an email will be sent to the customer.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="rnZVXhgPdNff">
        For
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         WISE
        </strong>
        rejected customers, they can still use SWIFT payment for outward transfers (USD, GBP, EUR) currencies only will be available.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="lGq7VL7Fq5lX">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT
        </strong>
        OR
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         WISE
        </strong>
        Transfers will be determined (based on currency)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="zxPfVRAqOyKs">
        WISE will still be available for
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
          sending
         </u>
        </strong>
        international transfer for other currencies except
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         (USD, EUR, GBP) and for available countries, refer to
        </strong>
        below links for more information about currency specific availability for each country.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="dtXzjDJDwNQB">
        Only refer to
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT
        </strong>
        available currencies
        <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="d4b274c7-488d-43cc-992d-b0241a55daac" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/Wio%20Personal%20-%20Send:%20Local%20&amp;%20International%20Payments/universal-transfers-and-payments-swift-wise-available-currencies-and-limits.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
         Universal - Transfers: SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="BbzX5T9hLsdX">

<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7shPfJlnZ0ZV">
</p>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="480" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:480px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="K2mvc7G30hYd">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        SWIFT Payments
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="5Erx65e3QZjT">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
         Key points:
        </em>
       </strong>
      </p>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       We have 2 types of transaction limits i.e., one which is
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        source account
       </strong>
       payment limit and the other one is
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        destination
       </strong>
       currency limit.
       <br/>
      </p>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       If a customer wants to
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        make a payment in USD to a UAE bank account from their Wio USD account,
       </strong>
       they still need to
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        choose ‘International Payments’
       </strong>
       then proceed with the international payments flow, payment will be processed as a normal SWIFT payment (
       <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://wiobank.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/ADQFS/pages/552894469/Local+International+Transfers+Payment+Gateways-+Ops+FO#First-new-international-payment" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        First new international payment
       </a>
       )
       <br/>
       <br/>
       If the customer chooses
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Local payment from their USD accounts
       </strong>
       , they will only see
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        AED currency
       </strong>
       option available.
       <br/>
       <br/>
       List of available countries:
       <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="d4b274c7-488d-43cc-992d-b0241a55daac" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/Wio%20Personal%20-%20Send:%20Local%20&amp;%20International%20Payments/universal-transfers-and-payments-swift-wise-available-currencies-and-limits.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        Universal - Transfers: SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits
       </a>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="5EHn7CJzc1ZP">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Jx32OV3utOrf">
        Wio bank now have its own
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT
        </strong>
        for sending/receiving international payments.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="pDRPyjLOZ9rT">
        No onboarding will be required to use
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT
        </strong>
        , however, customer account needs to be fully activated.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="CvMXBzmOFNpM">
        SWIFT system will support the 3 major currencies
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         (USD, EUR, GBP)
        </strong>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xuV7p85bPBjW">
        Current
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         AED
        </strong>
        accounts or
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         multi-Currency
        </strong>
        accounts will have the same process to send a SWIFT transfer.
       </li>
      </ul>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="jLHnprgj3jjo">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="jhG1vVMp17LZ">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Correspondent bank fees for SWIFT transfers is 15.75 USD, EUR, GBP or AED 63
        </strong>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ZwTrG91T6cwl">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Wio transaction fee for Wio retail is AED 0 - Launch feature - subject to change
        </strong>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="R51bPbqhfdO4">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bx57jdxQH1vT">
        Normal TAT for outward SWIFT payment would be
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         3 - 5 working days.
        </strong>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="irNLFqnPpx89">
        WISE will still be available for
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
          sending
         </u>
        </strong>
        international payments for other currencies except
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         (USD, EUR,GBP) and for available countries, refer to
        </strong>
        <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="d4b274c7-488d-43cc-992d-b0241a55daac" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/Wio%20Personal%20-%20Send:%20Local%20&amp;%20International%20Payments/universal-transfers-and-payments-swift-wise-available-currencies-and-limits.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
         Universal - Transfers: SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits
        </a>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TBJWEd285nnz">
        Currency exchange rate is locked to 5 minutes per transaction.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="RH9oFcP8HBTP">
        SWIFT copies are sent to customers once payment is confirmed.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="QZljyTMx2N7z">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT
        </strong>
        OR
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         WISE
        </strong>
        payments will be determined (based on Account currency and currency)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="iMuJh6Nl371R">
        WISE will still be available for
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
          sending
         </u>
        </strong>
        international payments from the AED account only, and for other countries local currencies except
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         (USD, EUR,GBP, INR, SAR) and for available countries, refer to
        </strong>
        <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="d4b274c7-488d-43cc-992d-b0241a55daac" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/Wio%20Personal%20-%20Send:%20Local%20&amp;%20International%20Payments/universal-transfers-and-payments-swift-wise-available-currencies-and-limits.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
         Universal - Transfers: SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits
        </a>
       </li>
      </ul>
     </td>
    </tr>
   </tbody>
  </table>
 </div>

<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="0o35XhenjHJz">
 Sending an International Payment: New Payment/New Payee
</h2>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="n7FCjDV5rqk8">
 How to + Application Steps:
</h3>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="Rw7zSOljTHPG">
</p>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="480" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:480px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="TNNyDpnC1CTd">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        How to
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="RRpLWPpfPqWq">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="NwDSV7Dh6bfH">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Login
        </strong>
        to Wio application
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="7Sh5C0fn31fX">
        Click on
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         product hub
        </strong>
        then select ‘
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Send
        </strong>
        ’
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="fppzNFJyZPXC">
        Send funds (locally/Internationally) by clicking on
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="aPt3QrccRn7B">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Send money from:
         </strong>
         to choose the account (AED or multi-currency) and start initiating the payment.
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bBTXbJfvrMoN">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Send money to
         </strong>
         : Where you can
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Add
         </strong>
         a new payee or choose from one of the existing payees.
        </li>
       </ul>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bkhjjl13qY6N">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Select
        </strong>
        which
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         account
        </strong>
        you would like to send money from (AED or multicurrency)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="NTjXFUvTg7yr">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Choose Country
        </strong>
        (Available countries displayed are UAE + SWIFT + Wise applicable countries:
        <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="d4b274c7-488d-43cc-992d-b0241a55daac" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/Wio%20Personal%20-%20Send:%20Local%20&amp;%20International%20Payments/universal-transfers-and-payments-swift-wise-available-currencies-and-limits.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
         Universal - Transfers: SWIFT &amp; WISE Available Currencies and limits
        </a>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ed6bRNtFPXTQ">
         Wise sheet:
         <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1N4OXPTL9VwQbvMmz66UUUdyAS_euKiTObSORF-A3qFE/edit#gid=1340615662" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
          https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1N4OXPTL9VwQbvMmz66UUUdyAS_euKiTObSORF-A3qFE/edit#gid=1340615662
         </a>
        </li>
       </ul>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="u4SYTJTx65WX">
        Choose
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         currency
        </strong>
        and
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         amount
        </strong>
        to send
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1HtSvpJP3VOS">
        Currencies available will be
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         based on applicable countries &amp; currencies
        </strong>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Fr1T31fvJxRv">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Example 1:
         </strong>
         If customer wants to send money to India, they’ll be able to send (INR/USD/EUR/GBP - SWIFT or Wise)
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="BXunpspXRQd2">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Example 2
         </strong>
         : If customer selects UK/US, they will be able to send through SWIFT only
        </li>
       </ul>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xJH5PXqwZLP9">
        Application will display
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         payment amount review
        </strong>
        that includes:
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="FPUbf9DhLpHd">
        Payment portal: SWIFT/Wise - based on currency and country chosen.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Z0BHX7bXa3sv">
        Currency exchange rate
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="eJ3Crpg1vALD">
        Estimated time for payment to arrive.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xDbJALwLa8dF">
        Transfer fees (including VAT)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="fcLP25vRu0if">
        Choose the applicable
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Transfer Fees
        </strong>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="YVVD4NFObfBL">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          OUR (I'd like to pay all the fees)
         </strong>
        </li>
        <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="HPcZnHnVtnl5">
          Customer will pay for Wio transfer fees + Correspondent bank fees.
         </li>
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="toQ1VPBTtzQv">
          Payee will receive the
          <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
           <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
            exact
           </u>
          </strong>
          amount transferred.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="tutjvwuLdXNQ">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          SHA: (I'd like to pay my share of the fees)
         </strong>
        </li>
        <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1aNhRrf573Ww">
          Wio customer will pay Wio transfer fees.
         </li>
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="pDxR4Kr3phXE">
          Payee will pay for the correspondent bank's fees.
         </li>
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="VhNLNN1tQoUh">
          Payee will receive
          <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
           <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
            less
           </u>
          </strong>
          than the total amount sent.
         </li>
         <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Dxj95NG7dJTj">
          Total amount to be paid.
         </li>
        </ul>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="IXObRYFt7BOL">
         Note: if the payment will go through
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Wise
         </strong>
         , customer can click on
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          ‘Wise terms &amp; conditions’
         </strong>
         to download PDF file for Wise T&amp;S
        </li>
       </ul>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="FZLrr952mVNt">
        Click
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         next (to add payee flow)
        </strong>
        - this flow will be skipped if customer selects an existing payee from the list of contacts.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="JnPlZjrZdb9J">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Choose purpose of payment (POP)
        </strong>
        from the list
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="DKkP723tyVrQ">
        Add a
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         note
        </strong>
        to the payee (advise customer to avoid including special characters)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="p370FulHDKio">
        A
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         payment confirmation
        </strong>
        will be displayed, including (Payment details +Payee details + (Notes - optional)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="LhPVr9D3RJkv">
        Customer will need to
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         swipe to confirm
        </strong>
        the payment.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="rTgN1v72Cr2l">
        Before confirming a payment, customer can choose to
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         cancel
        </strong>
        their payment and
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         delete
        </strong>
        the (New payment details) or
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         save as a draft
        </strong>
        for later use.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="BQTZmglfFzGx">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         2 factor authentication (2FA)
        </strong>
        will be triggered (OTP/Face ID/Touch ID)
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="U78ncr8zS1qr">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         Confirmation
        </strong>
        message will be displayed
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         (Mabrook! payment in process of amount xx)
        </strong>
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TP7N9j8aTPhb">
        Customer can
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         review
        </strong>
        their payment from the transactions list.
       </li>
      </ul>
     </td>
    </tr>

</p>
<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="VpxZ7pD34Z4F">
 Local and International: Add/Delete Payee Flow
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="7lpDkNjTC3M6">
</p>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="Ru1jEzzWP3I5">
 Add Payee Flow
</h3>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="480" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:480px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="WuVlcoVQbibN">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        How to
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="JxL39tXHtJjl">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="oZfbERzdv1Lh">
        Add new payee flow is available only through Send option while initiating a payment.
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="p2p6PQJTbfFf">
        Payee details will be saved to contacts list even if the payment is not completed by customer was able to add payee details and see the confirmation.
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
      </p>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Payee details includes:
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="yVzD5UPzNppY">
        Payee type: Person/Business
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="XnF3wF150Zli">
        Payee name
       </li>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="f1lt57xXv5e8">
        Nickname &amp; Email (Optional)
       </li>
      </ul>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
      </p>
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Bank account details:
       </strong>
      </p>
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="X5XSLJHpkV61">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         For Wise:
        </strong>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="QQLMzAxl9GrR">
         Dynamic: based on currency and country, refer to Wise sheet for currency specific information and requirements
         <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1N4OXPTL9VwQbvMmz66UUUdyAS_euKiTObSORF-A3qFE/edit#gid=1340615662" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
          https://docs.google.com/spreadsheets/d/1N4OXPTL9VwQbvMmz66UUUdyAS_euKiTObSORF-A3qFE/edit#gid=1340615662
         </a>
         <br/>
        </li>
       </ul>
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="P7TBQZ7bprQT">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         For SWIFT:
        </strong>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="fv2RFPXhiFT7">
         IBAN or Account number (15-32 digits long)
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="HmgqFjNgpKCS">
         Swift code
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="JXhjrQQE1FvF">
         <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
          Recipient address:
         </strong>
         Country of residence + Post code + State/Region + Town/City + Street)
        </li>
       </ul>
      </ul>
     </td>
    </tr>
   </tbody>
  </table>
 </div>
</div>

<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="6RznvKDXN7uy">
 Delete Payee Flow
</h3>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="4dlfTvJ5Tg7l">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Deleting a beneficiary:
 </strong>
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="Yb9K1BfjWLZZ">
 (Editing an existing beneficiary is not available)
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="yP1dnD1LjVRx">
  Login to Wio Personal application, from Product hub, select 'send'
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="LrTqKrn3QAnX">
  Click on ‘View all' displayed next to 'contacts'.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="idFTFOHTBh3J">
  Select the payee to delete.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="rf7HPppcBlxx">
  Click on the Delete icon.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Vn6NipbpX7lx">
  Confirmation will be displayed to delete the beneficiary.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="zdHpNvwqO39n">
  Confirm by selecting ‘Yes, Delete' or 'No, Cancel.'
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="5I3V7CVRn3l7">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph align-center" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" data-text-align="center" id="HzRfHP7cTTgb">
 <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
  <img alt="image.png" class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="image.png" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="/collections/WIO PERSONAL/resources/image.png" style="width:603px" width="603"/>
 </span>

<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="Hwe0BtkDPDOu">
 In App Transactions Tracker
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="XcgjtvrjFxBr">
 We started rolling out SME transaction tracker on SME app, 10% is completed, we will keep opening it incrementally this week on SME and next week on Retail.
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="3FNIQXdr3vUP">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Expectation
 </strong>
 :
</p>
<ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="nF6dJ15VpLNl">
  This feature will be able to help customer with where the txn is stuck and whether it is credited or not.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="YNonpBifs7Yt">
  While we are getting the status updated till final mile i.e. credited to bene, but we have observed 40% of txn are going to the recipient banks which are not on GPI tracking and hence we dont get the confirmation on the last credit to customer, in such cases we are giving relevant details to customer on tracker.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="Mpbvl3NldPHr">
  Educational comms and FAQ to customer will be updated once the complete feature is rolled out on relevant customer segment .
 </li>
</ol>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="VYNTLJTryTGW">
</h3>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="Jx98Zb3TVmjP">
 Feature Description
</h3>
<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="hbZzrlFm5Blx">
 Transaction tracker for International Transfer
</h3>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="DRjd341xB39d">
  Once the transaction is initiated, we will show transaction tracker in the application transaction history.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="DylhY2XjpB8B">
  Customers will be able to track
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   Swift transactions for USD, EUR, GBP
  </strong>
  accounts
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ✅
  </strong>
 </li>
 <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="oVzWxppErMfn">
   Tracker is not available
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    for
   </strong>
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    wise payments
   </strong>
  </li>
 </ul>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ZwJtZWLNjOOH">
  With this feature, customers will be able to see the whereabouts of outward txn (initiated on Citi) directly on transaction history (details section).
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="jXX7Q5b9SduX">
  Customer will be able to see txn tracker for all the txn initiated after 16 Dec 2023
  <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
   <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/33bce0ef-61b5-4071-b0e2-5abfb118f20b" style="width:16px" width="16"/>
  </span>
  in transaction history.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xgTznUOORhfh">
  Every status have specific description, date, and sub-description against each status level.
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="D7TNxn1Tnff5">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="HlipNnrihRt1">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
   Overall, we will maintain 5 statuses for any international transaction:
  </u>
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="f8Xr7fHZJVop">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Processing
   </strong>
   : the status will remain till the transaction is out from our network i.e.
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    till
   </strong>
   Ack_receieved in swift
   <del class="ghq-card-content__strikethrough" data-ghq-card-content-type="STRIKETHROUGH" style="text-decoration:line-through">
    and Processing in Wise
   </del>
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bZ9rHNd1PktC">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Sent
   </strong>
   : once we get Ack_receieved in swift
   <del class="ghq-card-content__strikethrough" data-ghq-card-content-type="STRIKETHROUGH" style="text-decoration:line-through">
    and Processing in Wise
   </del>
   we change the status to Sent
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Z9yhE7W3pJNP">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Completed
   </strong>
   : once we have Acknowledgement on customer credit, we change the status to Completed.
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="9EJ9Hr95hLUt">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Canceled
   </strong>
   : if rejection happened before we remit the customer.
  </li>
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="hvB1R5VvHa5D">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Refunded
   </strong>
   : if rejection or refund happened after we debited the customer (in this case we need to link the reversed transaction reference to original transaction).
  </li>
 </ul>
</ul>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="217.5" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:217.5px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="l3MdbF9jx2hX">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         You may share the below video to customers over WhatsApp
        </strong>
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="rxALXRFLR1PN">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <a class="ghq-card-content__file" data-ghq-card-content-filename="" data-ghq-card-content-type="FILE" href="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/07ad2c85-3f7e-4d55-b274-7c998089153b" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
        Payments tracker v8.mp4
       </a>
       <br/>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
   </tbody>
  </table>
 </div>

<h3 class="ghq-card-content__small-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="SMALL_HEADING" id="MrPtZwDnZbvb">
 Status on Swift transactions:
</h3>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="SBS2bnkp4BB3">
 Source:
 <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://wiobank.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/PA/pages/957087758/Transaction+tracker#Feature-Description" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
  https://wiobank.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/PA/pages/957087758/Transaction+tracker#Feature-Description
 </a>
</p>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="272,250,338.99999999999994,338.99999999999994,338.99999999999994,217.5" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:272px"/>
    <col style="width:250px"/>
    <col style="width:338.99999999999994px"/>
    <col style="width:338.99999999999994px"/>
    <col style="width:338.99999999999994px"/>
    <col style="width:217.5px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="V5JrvFTPRHvY">
 SWIFT/Wise Copy Requests
</h1>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="true" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="379,100,150">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:379px"/>
    <col style="width:100px"/>
    <col style="width:150px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="4mdYfHjJm9ff">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="nnB55HA7lXHp">
        <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
         SWIFT Copy Feature
        </strong>
        :
        <br/>
       </li>
       <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="zhJnDwNpTzDt">
         Available in transaction history for all Wio customers.
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ftlLPyZ2dR7l">
         Customers can obtain SWIFT copies for old transactions.
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ntHswZr9v7X2">
         Applicable for Local, SWIFT, and Wise outward transactions.
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="tUXxYDqzdeLx">
         Correspondent bank details and UETR number included (only for SWIFT transactions).
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="dVAhBvDIO1H3">
         SWIFT copy available in transaction emails sent to customers (for all types: Wise, SWIFT, Local).
        </li>
        <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="jXLXFGoFJZd7">
         Customers must use the latest application release to access this feature.
        </li>
       </ul>
      </ul>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/3583a996-3e91-4afc-802a-acf26b43652b" style="width:220px" width="220"/>
       </span>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
   </tbody>
  </table>

<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="5QhVxYQ0JPdT">
 Payment advice vs SWIFT copy
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="9Aul397C5T60">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="RDrWaBdfGvJw">
 Key points:
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="X2d0vjtzblJh">
  A payment advice will now be sent via email to Wio customers upon completing a transaction, for international ‘SWIFT/WISE’ payments.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="nRhDOvWXS1mv">
  <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    payment advice is not to be considered as a swift copy,
   </strong>
  </em>
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Hr7Ll537Z3fB">
  If customers are requesting for a payment confirmation:
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="6dBcj99PI5BI">
  1st: Inform customers they can view the transaction details through Mobile application or Wio web.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="3bJablWHSAx4">
  Always guide/refer customers to download/view payment confirmation through email sent to their registered email address.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="33uPqC26X9xx">
  example of email sent for SWIFT copy.
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="77jXrnWjL6T3">
 SWIFT copies are for completed transactions and we can issue them manually if requested by customers
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  within 24 hours from payment completion date
 </strong>
 (current process) - steps below)
</p>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-is-full-width="false" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="350,363,320" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:350px"/>
    <col style="width:363px"/>
    <col style="width:320px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="hBJ9lleS67N9">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        SWIFT copy (MT 103)
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">

    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="65bNebXXDxIK">

       <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="53TDnr9v3Z34">

      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       Any questions? Please contact us on 600 500 946 or email
       <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="mailto:care@wio.io">
        care@wio.io
       </a>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">

<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="mRtz87fNpJtF">
 WISE payments Copy Requests
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="f9jTwgbRJZvz">
</p>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="TqDbfLNn1wvu">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Key Points:
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="v7thdZ9dmR9x">
  Wio Care can raise the case to BO payments team for wise related issues like reason for return of funds, status of payment etc.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="t1lX9Drn5zRD">
  BO will email Wise to advise further.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="TpHbDPLpD5bz">
  Once update is received, same will be shared with FO.
 </li>

       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">

       </strong>

       <br/>

       <br/>

       <br/>
       <br/>
       -
       <br/>

       <br/>

       <br/>
       <br/>
       -

       </strong>
       Everyday banking Queue through ThinkOwl and post through Slack channel:
       <a class="ghq-card-content__link" data-ghq-card-content-type="LINK" href="https://wiobank.slack.com/archives/C04UW8CHSCS" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">

<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="t3N5zERRvrFD">
 FX margin
</h2>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="680">

      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Key Points:
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       Sheet shows the different FX for both standard and plus plan
       <br/>
       <br/>
       Buying = Outward
       <br/>
       <br/>
       Selling = Inward
       <br/>
       <br/>
       This is an internal sheet - here’s what you
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        can
       </strong>
       /
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        cant'
       </strong>
       share with customers:
       <br/>

       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        can share
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       -
       <br/>
       USD outward FX margin for standard and plus →
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        can share
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       -
       <br/>
       Outward EUR. GBP, SAR, INR FX margin for standard and plus plans →
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        can’t share
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       -
       <br/>
       Inward EUR. GBP, SAR, INR FX margin for standard and plus plans →
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        can’t share
       </strong>
      </p>

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="NShFrvxN3gKt">
 Purpose of Payment (POP) Codes
</h1>
<div class="ghq-card-content__table-responsive-wrapper">
 <div class="ghq-card-content__table-scroller">
  <table class="ghq-card-content__table" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE" data-ghq-table-column-widths="480,150,217.5" data-ghq-table-header="true">
   <colgroup>
    <col style="width:480px"/>
    <col style="width:150px"/>
    <col style="width:217.5px"/>
   </colgroup>
   <tbody class="ghq-card-content__table-body">
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="05IbShnSl4u3">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Key Points
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        Local Payments POP Codes
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        International Payments POP Codes
       </strong>
      </p>
     </td>
    </tr>
    <tr class="ghq-card-content__table-row" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_ROW" id="PliePVrrAzPO">
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       The List and codes can be shared with customers, however:
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/d121e917-477f-43bb-91a0-0ae4163b98e9" style="width:16px" width="16"/>
       </span>
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        NEVER suggest a specific code for customers to enter as it will be considered as tipping off
       </strong>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/d121e917-477f-43bb-91a0-0ae4163b98e9" style="width:16px" width="16"/>
       </span>
       <br/>
       What is a purpose of payment code:
       <br/>
       <br/>
       POP codes are
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        uniform code list with three-digit codes to determine the purpose of all incoming and outgoing transfers
       </strong>
       . Please note, if a valid Purpose of Payment code is not provided, payment(s) may get rejected or delayed.
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <br/>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/434c39c0-84b3-4ce5-a202-75e67c5015fc" style="width:150px" width="150"/>
       </span>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/82cb607b-2bf4-4de7-b65f-a53b741e939e" style="width:150px" width="150"/>
       </span>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/d6565aed-f081-442e-b188-b0aef23760fc" style="width:150px" width="150"/>
       </span>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/82119d68-c377-4602-9a67-003de4c449c1" style="width:150px" width="150"/>
       </span>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/e19b54f7-f9ea-4fcf-9cf2-20755f312431" style="width:150px" width="150"/>
       </span>
      </p>
     </td>
     <td class="ghq-card-content__table-cell" data-ghq-card-content-type="TABLE_CELL">
      <p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph">
       <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
        <em class="ghq-card-content__italic" data-ghq-card-content-type="ITALIC">
         <u class="ghq-card-content__underline" data-ghq-card-content-type="UNDERLINE" style="text-decoration:underline">
          International Payments (Business)
         </u>
        </em>
       </strong>
       <br/>
       <span class="ghq-card-content__image-container">
        <img class="ghq-card-content__image" data-ghq-card-content-image-filename="Unnamed" data-ghq-card-content-type="IMAGE" src="https://content.api.getguru.com/files/view/cfb89a98-e00a-405d-a6cf-22d27d24e1df" style="width:150px" width="150"/>

<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="BB9rJvjNLisT">
 The UAE Payment Gateway System (UAEPGS)
</h1>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="tZ5VR9Tvd6TO">
  Wio does not currently support UAEPGS Payment Gateway system for transactions.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="yvn9L5Te1g3N">
  For instance, when a customer uses the exchange application (Al Ansari exchange, Al Fardan Exchange, ETC……) , they are redirected to the bank's web portal through UAEPGS system. Upon logging in, the customer authorizes the payment, resulting in the deduction of the specified amount from their account.
 </li>
</ul>
<hr class="ghq-card-content__horizontal-rule" data-ghq-card-content-type="DIVIDER"/>
<h1 class="ghq-card-content__large-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="LARGE_HEADING" id="x3Z5D4zFlJ7x">
 Possible Error Codes and technical issues
</h1>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="FMjDtLq5PFDk">
</h2>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="PRhLaIxlSS11">
 Customer Not Receiving Funds
</h2>
<ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="UhLNdTkAZfnt">
  Check with sender bank (Amount might be on hold)
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="XjB3WpB5azfF">
  If less than 3-5 working days advise customer to wait
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="rZZLzQ38dlJ3">
  Ask them for
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT copy.
  </strong>
 </li>
 <ol class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST" start="1">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="5iKvwnADlt37">
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    SWIFT copy:
   </strong>
   a confirmation of the payment made from your bank and includes all the details of your transaction including date, amount, currency, sender, recipient and any fees applied.
  </li>
 </ol>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__numbered-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="NUMBERED_LIST_ITEM" id="ZrdjPWjMZw9K">
  Assign case to
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   SWIFT Payments or Wise payment queries (whichever applicable)
  </strong>
 </li>
</ol>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="0dirbMVTtW65">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="gj6pxRTe7dP4">
 Possible Technical Issues
</h2>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="teXoW3pxYjVF">
  Customer is unable to see
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ‘Save Payee’
  </strong>
  option after saving needed details:
 </li>
 <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="ULmbUvwRBXwl">
   Ask Customer to fill all
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    mandatory
   </strong>
   details for the application to display next step, that’s how application logic works.
  </li>
 </ul>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Hcv1MFkvsLpE">
  Customer is getting
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   ‘payment failed’
  </strong>
  error message:
 </li>
 <ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
  <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xNZ9DGjEhrTn">
   Ask customer to avoid using any
   <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
    Numbers and special characters (!@#$%^&amp;*/,)
   </strong>
   then try again.
  </li>
 </ul>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="bjhmknLfjPI5">
  <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
   For other technical inquiries, refer to:
  </strong>
  <a class="ghq-card-content__guru-card" data-ghq-card-content-type="GURU_CARD" data-ghq-guru-card-id="9febb4fc-ae8b-4175-af7b-c95caedd550e" href="https://github.com/RabboPasch/guru-to-github/blob/main/collections/WIO%20PERSONAL/%F0%9F%91%A8%F0%9F%8F%BC%E2%80%8D%F0%9F%92%BBUniversal%20-%20Handling%20Tech%20Issues%20Reported%20by%20Customers/universal-handling-tech-issues-reported-by-customers.md" rel="noopener noreferrer" target="_blank">
   👨🏼‍💻Universal - Handling Tech Issues Reported by Customer
  </a>
 </li>
</ul>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph ghq-is-empty" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="XFQZ9bd8clRv">
</p>
<h2 class="ghq-card-content__medium-heading" data-ghq-card-content-type="MEDIUM_HEADING" id="9qBLRc99WaxR">
 List of transfer related error codes
</h2>
<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="uvzsyzaTT11j">
 <strong class="ghq-card-content__bold" data-ghq-card-content-type="BOLD">
  Below errors are not to be considered as technical errors, and we can guide customers based on their situation.
 </strong>
</p>
<ul class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST">
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="95XLpvpNhVL9">
  Duplicate nickname
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="Em6Bv7jPTkxJ">
  Wrong email format for adding payee.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="pHH6f59xVDHp">
  IBAN is empty.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="1veA71rbrdgP">
  Confirm IBAN doesn’t match.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="FRL5XZDr6TJN">
  Not completed all payee info when saving
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xJBSQJ1Sbvvj">
  Transfer amount is empty.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="BTZjyxhLH1D3">
  No payment purpose selected.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="xn93HrN5TbEN">
  Exceeding transfer limit
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="059jblzcqVfi">
  Only English alphabet is allowed.
 </li>
 <li class="ghq-card-content__bulleted-list-item" data-ghq-card-content-type="BULLETED_LIST_ITEM" id="VxrHZvFD95fb">
  Special characters are not allowed.
 </li>
</ul>

<p class="ghq-card-content__paragraph" data-ghq-card-content-type="paragraph" id="5LAT5vcP84VR">
